sadya evādya mugdhā tad aghadamanavaktrodgīrṇatāmbūlam alpaṃsphuṭam aviditam āsye nyastam asyās tvayāli  RUnm gandhād yathāvibhrājante kva sakhi sukhinaḥ śākhino mohanās teyeṣāṃ puṣpair iyam anupamā vaijayantī kṛtāsti paśyākṛṣṭabhramarapaṭalā yātayāmāpi kāmaṃyā bhūyobhir mama parimalaiḥ stambhayaty adya cetaḥ  RUnm lokottarapadārthānāṃ prabhāvaḥ kopy anargalaḥ ratiṃ tadviṣayaṃ cāsau bhāsayet tūrṇam ekadā  RUnm atha sambandhaḥsambandhaḥ kularūpādisāmagrīgauravaṃ bhavet  RUnm tato yathāvīryaṃ kandukitādirrūpam akhilakṣmāmaṇḍalīmaṇḍanaṃjanmābhīrapurandarasya bhavane pāreparārdhaṃ guṇāḥ līlā kvāpi jagaccamatkṛtikarīty etasya lokottarāvṛttir veṇudharasya durmukhi dhṛtiṃ kasyāḥ kṣaṇaṃ rakṣati  RUnm atha abhimānaḥsantu ramyāṇi bhūrīṇi prārthyaṃ syād idam eva me iti yo nirṇayo dhīrair abhimānaḥ sa ucyate  RUnm tato yathāsphurantu bahavaḥ kṣitau madhurimormidhaureyakāvidagdhamaṇayo guṇāvalipatiṃvarābhir vṛtāḥ na yasya śikhicandraṃ śirasi naiva veṇur mukhena dhātuvacanā tanau sakhi tṛṇāya manye na tam  RUnm atha tadīyaviśeṣāḥtadīyānāṃ viśeṣāḥ syuḥ padagoṣṭhapriyādayaḥ  RUnm tatra padānipadāny atra padāṅkāḥ syuḥ  RUnm tato yathāsphurati sakhi rathāṅgāmbhojadambholibhājāṃtaṭabhuvi viśadeyaṃ kasya paṅktiḥ padānām hṛdayam aghṛṇaghūrṇāghrātam udghāṭayantīmama tanulatikāyāṃ kuḍmalaṃ yā tanoti  RUnm atha goṣṭhamgoṣṭhaṃ vṛndāvanāśritam  RUnm tato yathāmadayati hṛdayaṃ sakhi vrajoyaṃmadhurimabhiḥ kvacid apy adṛṣṭapūrvaiḥ iha viharati kopi nāgarendarastribhuvanamaṇḍalamūrtir ity avehi  RUnm atha priyajanaḥprauḍhabhāvānubiddho yas tasya priyajanotra saḥ  RUnm tato yathāgurubhir niṣiddhā tām ahaṃ yāvad akṣṇoḥpadam anayamanantaśreyasāṃ sadma rādhām tṛṣitam iva mano me prekṣate tanvi tāvaddiśi diśi viharantīṃ śyāmalāṃ śālabhañjīm  RUnm atha upamāyathā kathañcid apy asya sādṛśyam upamoditā  RUnm tato yathānavāmbudharamādhurī sphurati mūrtir urvītalekṛśodari dṛśor iyāt pathi kim īdṛśo vā yuvā puraḥ sumukhi gopateḥ sadai sanniviṣṭasya mepitur vitanute naṭo yam anukṛtya nṛtyakramam  RUnm yathā vāsphuraty eṣa preyān iva navaghanas tasya subhageśikhaṇḍīnāṃ śreṇīṃ tulayati surendrāyudham idam asau vāso lakṣmīr iva viharate vidyud iti sāniśamyodasrākṣī tvayi nihitabuddhir nivasati  RUnm atha svabhāvaḥbhair hetvanapekṣī tu svabhāvorthaḥ prakīrtitaḥ nisargaś ca svarūpaṃ cety eṣopi bhavati dvidhā  RUnm atra nisargaḥnisargaḥ sudṛḍhābhyāsajanyaḥ saṃskara ucyate tadudbhodhasya hetuḥ syād guṇarūpaśrutir manāk  RUnm tato yathāsa tarjatu batāgrajaṃ tyajatu māṃ suhṛnmaṇḍalaḥpitā kila vilajjatāṃ ghanadṛgambur ambāstu me manaḥ sakhi samīhate śrutaguṇaśriyaṃ sarvathātam eva yadupuṅgavaṃ na tu kadāpi caidyaṃ nṛpam  RUnm yathā vāasundaraḥ sundaraśekharo vāguṇair vihīno guṇināṃ varo vā dveṣī mayi syāt karuṇāmbudhir vāśyāmaḥ sa evādya gatir mamāyam  RUnm atha svarūpamajanyas tu svataḥsiddhaḥ svarūpaṃ bhāva iṣyate etat tu kṛṣṇalalanobhayaniṣṭhatayā tridhā  RUnm atha kṛṣṇaniṣṭhamkṛṣṇaniṣṭhaṃ svarūpaṃ syād adaityaiḥ sugamaṃ janaiḥ  RUnm tato yathāiyaṃ vyaktir gopī na bhavati puraḥ kintu kutukīharir nārīveśo yad akhilasurastrīr dhuvati naḥ jagannetraśreṇītimiraharaṇāyāmbaramaṇiṃvinā kasyānyasya priyasakhi bhaved aupayikatā  RUnm atha lalanāniṣṭhamsvarūpaṃ lalanāniṣṭhaṃ svayam udbuddhatāṃ vrajet adṛṣṭepy aśrutepy uccaiḥ kṛṣṇe kuryād drutaṃ ratim  RUnm tato yathājihīte yaḥ kakṣāṃ kvacid alam adṛṣṭāśrutacaratrilokyām astīti kṣaṇam api na sambhāvanamayīm ghanaśyāmaṃ pītāmbaram ahaha saṅkalpayad amuṃjanaṃ kañcid goṣṭhe sakhi mama vṛthā dīryati manaḥ  RUnm atha ubhayaniṣṭhamtat syād ubhayaniṣṭhaṃ yat svarūpaṃ kṛṣṇasubhruvoḥ  RUnm tato yathā lalitamādhave sahacari harir eṣa brahmaveśaṃ prapannaḥkim ayam itarathā me vidravaty antarātmā śaśadharamaṇivedī svedadhārāṃ prasūtena kila kumudabandhoḥ kaumudīm antareṇa  RUnm proktā atrābhiyogādyā vilāsādhikyahetave ratiḥ svabhāvajaiva syāt prāyo gokulasubhruvām  RUnm sādhāraṇī nigaditā samañjasāsau samarthā ca kubjādiṣu mahiṣīṣu ca gokuladevīṣṇḍ ca kramataḥ  RUnm maṇivaccintāmaṇivatkaustubhamaṇivat tridhābhimatā nātisulabheyam abhitaḥ sudurlabhā syād ananyalabhyā ca  RUnm tatra sādhāraṇīnātisāndrā hareḥ prāyaḥ sākṣād darśanasambhavā sambhogecchānidāneyaṃ ratiḥ sādhāraṇī matā  RUnm yathā śrīdaśame sahoṣyatām iha preṣṭha dināni katicin mayā ramasva notsahe tyaktuṃ saṅgaṃ temburuhekṣaṇa  RUnm asāndratvād rater asyāḥ sambhogecchā vibhidyate etasyā hrāsato hrāsas taddhetutvād rater api  RUnm atha samañjasāpatnībhāvābhimānātmā guṇādiśravaṇādijā kvacid bheditasambhogatṛṣṇā sāndrā samañjasā  RUnm yathā tatraiva kā tvā mukunda mahatī kulaśīlarūpavidyāvayodraviṇadhāmabhir ātmatulyam dhīrā patiṃ kulavatī na vṛṇīta kanyākāle nṛsiṃha naralokamanobhirāmam  RUnm samañjasātaḥ sambhogaspṛhāyā bhinnatā yadā tadā tadutthitair bhāvair vaśyatā duṣkarā hariḥ  RUnm tathā hi tatraiva smāyāvalokalavadarśitabhāvahāribhrūmaṇḍalaprahitasauratamantraśauṇḍaiḥ patnyas tu ṣoḍaśasahasram anaṅgabāṇairyasyendriyaṃ vimathituṃ karaṇair na śekuḥ  RUnm atha samarthākaṃcid viśeṣam āyantyā sambhogecchā yayābhitaḥ ratyā tādātmyam āpannā sā samartheti bhaṇyate  RUnm svasvarūpāt tadīyād vā jātā yatkiṃcidanvayāt samarthā sarvavismārigandhā sāndratamā matā  RUnm prekṣyāśeṣe jagati madhurāṃ svāṃ vadhūṃ śaṅkayā tetasyāḥ pārśve gurubhir abhitas tvatprasaṅgo nyavāri śrutvā dūre tad api bhavataḥ sā tulākoṭinādaṃhā kṛṣṇety aśrutacaram api vyāharanty unmadāsīt  RUnm sarvādbhutavilāsormicamatkārakaraśriyaḥ sambhogecchāviśeṣosyā rater jātu na bhidyate ity asyāṃ kṛṣṇasaukhyārtham eva kevalam udyamaḥ  RUnm pūrvasyāṃ svasukhāyāpi kadācit tatra sambhavet  RUnm iyam eva ratiḥ prauḍhā mahābhāvadaśāṃ vrajet yā mṛgyā syād vimuktānāṃ bhaktānāṃ ca varīyasām  RUnm yathā śrīdaśame etāḥ paraṃ tanubhṛto bhuvi gopavadhvogovinda eva nikhilātmani rūḍhabhāvāḥ vāñchanti yad bhavabhiyo munayo vayaṃ cakiṃ brahmajanmabhir anantakathārasasya  RUnm syād dṛḍheyaṃ ratiḥ premā prodyan snehaḥ kramād ayam syān mānaḥ praṇayo rāgonurāgo bhāva ity api  RUnm bījam ikṣuḥ sa ca rasaḥ sa guḍaḥ khaṇḍa eva saḥ sa śarkarā sitā sā ca sā yathā syāt sitopalā  RUnm ataḥ premavilāsāḥ syur bhāvāḥ snehādayas tu ṣaṭ prāyo vyavahiryantemī premaśabdena sūribhiḥ  RUnm yasyā yādṛśajātīyaḥ kṛṣṇe premābhyudañcati tasyāṃ tādṛśajātīyaḥ sa kṛṣṇasyāpy udīyate  RUnm tatra premāsarvathā dhvaṃsarahitaṃ saty api dhvaṃsakāraṇe yadbhāvabandhanaṃ yūnoḥ sa premā parikīrtitaḥ  RUnm yathāśape tubhyaṃ dharmasthitimanyusarantyā sakhi mayāviśuddhām ugrābhir muhur api nirasto bhaṇitibhiḥ sa mugdhe śyāmātmā tyajati na hi me vartma bata māṃjagārāpadghorā viracayatu śāstiṃ gṛhapatiḥ  RUnm yathā vārādhāyāḥ sakhi sadguṇair anudinaṃ rūpānurāgādibhiḥsāndrāṃ labdhavator api vyasanitāṃ vyākṣiptakāntāntaraiḥ prāpa kvāpi parasparopari yayor na mlānatāṃ yas tayostaṃ candrāvalicandrakābharaṇayoḥ ko vetti bhāvakramam  RUnm sa tridhā kathyate prauḍhamadhyamandaprabhedataḥ  RUnm tatra prauḍhaḥvilambādibhir ajñātacittavṛttau priye jane itarakleśakārī yaḥ sa premā prauḍha ucyate  RUnm yathāgatvā brūhi nikuñjasadmani sakhe khinnāṃ mama preyasīṃmā kālātyayam ākalayya kamale mayy apratītiṃ kṛthāḥ duṣṭaṃ dānavam atra gokulaśiraḥśūlaṃ cikitsann ahaṃdrāg eṣa praṇayena pallavamayīṃ labdhosmi śayyāṃ tava  RUnm atha madhyaḥitarānubhavāpekṣāṃ sahate yaḥ sa madhyamaḥ  RUnm yathāsarvārambhamanoharāṃ sapadi me candrāvalīṃ vindatoraṅgaḥ śāradaśarvarīsamucitaḥ paryāptim evāyayau tāṃ kandarpacamūcamatkṛtikarakrīḍormikirmīritāṃrādhāṃ hanta tathāpi cittam adhunā sākṣān mamāpekṣate  RUnm atha mandaḥsadā paricitatvādeḥ karoty atyantikāt tu yaḥ naivopekṣāṃ na cāpekṣāṃ sa premā manda ucyate  RUnm yathāanumīya rūḍhamānām ānaya bhāmāṃ sakhīm aśokalatām bhavati premavatīnāṃ manāg upekṣāpi doṣāya  RUnm athavāprauḍhaḥ premā sa yatra syād viśleṣasyāsahiṣṇutā  RUnm yathā uddhavasandeśe nirmāya tvaṃ vitara phalakam hāri kaṃsārimūrtyāvāraṃ vāraṃ diśasi yadi māṃ mānanirvāhanāya yat paśyantī bhavanakuhare ruddhakarṇāntarāhaṃsāhaṃkārā priyasakhi sukham yāpayiṣyāmi yāmam  RUnm kṛcchrāt sahiṣṇutā yatra sa tu madhyama ucyate  RUnm yathāavitatham asau kiṃ drāghīyān gamiṣyati vāsaraḥsumukhi sa niśārambhaḥ kiṃvā sameṣyati maṅgalaḥ smitamukhaśaśī godhūlibhiḥ karambitakuntalaḥkṣapayati dṛśām ārtiṃ yatra vrajeśvaranandanaḥ  RUnm sa mandaḥ kathito yatra bhavet kutrāpi vismṛtiḥ  RUnm yathāpratipakṣajanerṣyayā na mesmṛtir āsīd vanamālyagumphane sakhi kiṃ karavai gavāṃ puroghanahambādhvanir eṣa jṛmbhate  RUnm atha snehaḥāruhya paramāṃ kāṣṭhāṃ premā ciddīpadīpanaḥ hṛdayaṃ drāvayann eṣa sneha ity abhidhīyate atrodite bhavej jātu na tṛptir darśanādiṣu  RUnm yathā kramadīpikāyām tad atimadhurarūpakamraśobhāmṛtarasapānavidhānalālasābhyām praṇayasalilapūravāhinīnāmalasavilolavilocanāmbujābhyām  RUnm yathā vājyotsnaśīdhuṃ harimukhavidhor apy analpaṃ pibantaunāntas tṛptiṃ tava katham api prāpnuto dṛkcakorau āghūrṇantau madakalatayā suṣṭhu mugdhau yad etaubhūyo bhūyas tam iha vamato bāṣpapūracchalena  RUnm aṅgasaṅge viloke ca śravaṇādau ca sa kramāt kaniṣṭho madhyamaḥ śreṣṭhas trividhoyaṃ manodravaḥ  RUnm tatra aṅgasaṅge yathāasi ghanarasarūpas tvaṃ pālī lāvaṇyasāramayamūrtiḥ mādhava bhavadāśleṣe bhavitā nāsyāḥ kathaṃ dravatā  RUnm viloke yathāasyās tvadvadane sarojasuhṛdi vyaktiṃ purastād gatenāścaryaṃ dravatām avindata manohaiyaṅgavīnaṃ yadi kintv āścaryam idaṃ mukunda milite śyāmāmukhendau bhavaccetaś candramaṇir dravan jalatayā bhūyo babhūvācalaḥ  RUnm śravaṇe yathāśrutiparisarakakṣāṃ yāti nāmnas tavārdhemuradamana dṛgambhodārayā dhautagātrī madanamadamadhūlīmugdhamedhāsamṛddhiḥskhalati kuvalayākṣī jṛmbhate stambhate ca  RUnm ādiśabdena smaraṇe yathākṛṣṇavartmani kṛtābhiniveśosāmprataḥ tvam asi kampitagātrī snehapūraparipākamayaṃ tekiṃ bhaviṣyati mano na vilīnam  RUnm sa ghṛtaṃ madhu cetyuktaṃ sneho dvedhā svarūpataḥ  RUnm tatra ghṛtasnehaḥātyantikādaramayaḥ sneho ghṛtam itīryate  RUnm bhāvāntarānvitao gacchan svādodrekaṃ na tu svayam ghanībhaven nisargātiśītalān mitha ādarāt gāḍhādaramayas tena snehaḥ syād ghṛtavad ghṛtam  RUnm yathāabhutthāya vidūrato madhubhñdā yāśliṣyate sādaraṃyā snehena vaśīkaroti guruṇā pāvitryapūrṇena tam kṣipraṃ yāti sitopaleva vilayaṃ tatkelivṛṣṭyā ca yāyuktā hanta kayopamātum api sā candrāvalī me sakhī  RUnm yathā vānijam agharipuṇāṃse nyastam ākṛṣya savyaṃbhujam iha nidadhānā dakṣam asrokṣitākṣī padayugam api baṅkaṃ śaṅkayā vikṣipantīpratiyuvativayasyāṃ smerayāmāsa gaurī  RUnm ādaro gauravotthaḥ syād ity anyonyāśritadvayam ratyādau sad api snehe suvyaktatvād ihocyate  RUnm madīyatātiśayabhāk priye sneho bhaven madhu svayaṃ prakaṭamādhuryo nānārasasamāhṛtiḥ  RUnm mattatoṣmadharaḥ sneho madhusāmyān madhūcyate  RUnm yathārādhā snehamayena hanta racitā mādhuryasāreṇa sāsaudhīva pratimā ghanāpy uruguṇair bhāvoṣmaṇā vidrutā yannāmany api dhāmani śravaṇayor yāti prasaṅgena mesāndrānandamayī bhavaty anupamā sadyo jagadvismṛti  RUnm atha mānaḥsnehas tūtkṛṣṭatāvāptyā mādhuryaṃ mānayan navam yo dhārayaty adākṣiṇyaṃ sa māna iti kīrtyate  RUnm yathāsravadasrabhare kṛte dṛśau metava godhūlibhir eva gopavīra adhunā vadanānilaiḥ kim ebhirvirameti bhrūkuṭiṃ babhāra subhrūḥ  RUnm udātto lalitaś ceti mānoyaṃ dvividho mataḥ  RUnm tatra udāttaḥudāttaḥ syād ghṛtasneho dhārayan gahanakramam dākṣiṇyabhāgadākṣiṇyaṃ vāmyagandhaṃ ca kutracit  RUnm tatra dākṣiṇyodātto yathārādheti skhilābhidhe mayi haṭhād biddhāntarāpy ārtibhirmadvailakṣyaśamāya sā dviguṇayanty āsyāravinde smitam jalpe ca mradimānubiddham adhikaṃ mādhuryam ātanvatīcitrāṇīva cakāra matpriyasuhṛdvṛnāni candrāvalī  RUnm atha vāmyagandhodāttoyathā śrīviṣṇupurāṇe kācid bhrūbhaṅguraṃ kṛtvā lalāṭaphalakaṃ harim vilokya netrabhṛṅgābhyāṃ papau tanmukhapaṅkajam  RUnm yathā vāakṣasaṃsadi jitāpi mṛgākṣīmādhavena parirambhapaṇena bhugnadṛṣṭir iha vipratipannāṃtaṃ karaṇe rurudhe pariripsum  RUnm atha lalitaḥmadhusnehas tu kauṭilyaṃ svātantryahṛdayaṅgamam bibhrannarmaviśeṣaṃ ca lalitoyam udīryate  RUnm tatra kauṭilyalalitoyathā śrīdaśame ekā bhrūkuṭim ābaddhya premasaṃrambhavihvalā ghnatīvaikṣat sandaṣṭadaśanacchadā  RUnm yathā vāadatta me vartmani manmathonmadāsvayaṃgrahāśleṣam asau sakhī tava ity uktavantaṃ kuṭilībhavan mukhīkṛṣṇaṃ vataṃsena jaghāna maṅgalā  RUnm yathā vācitraṃ cirasparśasukhāya cucukekurvantam akṣipram iyaṃ calekṣaṇā svinnāṅgulīkaṃ pulakāñcitaśriyāsavyena cikṣepa kucena keśavam  RUnm atha narmalalitoyathā dānakelikaumudyām mithyā jalpatu te kathaṃ nu rasanā sādhvīsahasrasya yābimboṣṭhāmṛtasevanād agharipo puṇyā prayatnād abhūt kasmād eva balṃtkarotu ca karaḥ soḍhuṃ kṣamaḥ subhruvāṃraktaḥ suṣṭhu na nIvibandham api yaḥ kā vānyabandhe kathā  RUnm atha praṇayaḥmāno dadhāno viśrambhaṃ praṇayaḥ procyate budhaiḥ  RUnm yathākucopānte spṛṣṭā muravijayinā tadbhujaśirastironyastagrīvā bhruvam anṛjudṛṣṭir vibhujatī paṭenāsya mlānīkṛtapuraṭabhāsā pulakinīpramodāsrair dhautaṃ nijamukham iyaṃ mārṣṭi sumukhī  RUnm svarūpaṃ praṇayasyāsya viśrambhaḥ kathito budhaiḥ viśrambhopi dvidhā maitraṃ sakhyaṃ ceti nigadyate  RUnm tatra maitraṃbhāvajñaiḥ procyate maitraṃ viśrambho vinayānvitaḥ  RUnm yathā śrīdaśame kācit karāmbujaṃ śaurer jagṛheñjalināṃ mudā kācid dadhāra tadbāhum aṃse candanarūṣitam  RUnm yathā vāna hi saṅkuca paṅkajekṣaṇaḥpādayos te nidadhātu nūpurau anayor dhvanibhir vilajjatāṃkalahaṃsīva vipakṣakāminī  RUnm atha sakhyamvisrambhaṃ sādhvasonmuktaḥ sakhyaṃ svavaśatāmayaḥ  RUnm yathāsarabhasam adhikaṇṭham arpitābhyāṃdanujaripor nijabāhuvallarībhyām niṭilam avanamayya tasya karṇesakhi kathitaṃ kim iva tvayā rahasyam  RUnm yathā vā śrīviṣṇupurāṇe yadi te tadvacaḥ satyaṃ satyātyarthaṃ priyeti me madgehaniṣkuṭārthāya tadāyaṃ nīyatāṃ taruḥ  RUnm yathā vāvinyasya vakṣoruhakorakadvayīṃvakṣaḥsthale kaṃsaharasya hāriṇīm patrāṅkuraṃ kuṅkumabindunālikelikhaty asau candramukhī sakhī mama  RUnm yathā vā śrīdaśame tato gatvā vanoddeśe dṛptā keśavam abravīt na pārayehaṃ calituṃ naya māṃ yatra te manaḥ  RUnm janitvā praṇayaḥ snehāt kutracin mānatāṃ vrajet snehān mānaḥ kvacid bhūtvā praṇayatvam athāśnute  RUnm kāryakāraṇatānyonnyam ataḥ praṇayamānayoḥ ity atra pṛthag evāsau viśrambhodāhṛtiḥ kṛtā  RUnm udāttalalitābhyāṃ tu maitryasakhye susaṅgate dve sumaitryasusakhyākhye yathāsaṅkhyam udīrite  RUnm tatra sumaitryamālīpuraḥ kathayituṃ rajanīrahasyaṃtatrodyate madhuripau mṛdulā bhramadbhrūḥ utkṣipya tan mukhapuṭāvaraṇāya hastaṃnyañcanmukhī samavariṣṭa punar varākṣī  RUnm yathā vākṣipte varṇakabhājane taraṇijāpure parīhāsataḥkṛṣṇena bhruvam āracayya kuṭilām ālokayantī tiraḥ tārā vakṣasi citram ardhalikhitaṃ śrīvatsavibhrājitekāśmīreṇa ghanaśriyā nijakucākṛṣṭena pūrṇaṃ vyadhāt  RUnm atha susakhyamdyūte sakṛt pānavidhau paṇīkṛtejitvā dviroṣṭhaṃ pibati svam acyute babandha kaṇṭhe kuṭilīkṛtekṣaṇātaṃ vāmayā dorlatayāsya vallavī  RUnm yathā vāāviṣkurvati visphuran navanakhollekhaṃ svavakṣastaṭaṃkṛṣṇe pītadukūlasaṅkalanayā smitvā sakhīnāṃ puraḥ abhraśyāmam uro rurodha valitabhrūr ānanaṃ dhunvatīromāñcodgamakañcukena kucayor dvandvena gāndharvikā  RUnm atha rāgaḥduḥkham apy adhikaṃ citte sukhatvenaiva rajyate yatas tu praṇayotkarṣāt sa rāga iti kīrtyate  RUnm yathātīvrārkadyutidīpitair asilatādhārākarālāsribhirmārtaṇḍopalamaṇḍalaiḥ sthapuṭitepy adres taṭe tasthuṣī paśyanti paśupendranandanam asāv indīvarair āstṛtetalpe nyastapadāmbujeva muditā na spandate rādhikā  RUnm yathā vā padyāvalyāṃ tārābhisāraka caturthaniśāśaśāṅkakāmāmburāśiparivardhana deva tubhyam argho namo bhavatu me saha tena yūnāmithyāpavādavacasāpy abhimānasiddhiḥ  RUnm nīlimā raktimā ceti rāgoyaṃ dvividho mataḥ  RUnm tatra nīlimānīlīśyāmābhavo rāgo nīlimā kathyate budhaiḥ  RUnm tatra nīlīrāgaḥvyayasambhāvanāhīno bahir nātiprakāśavān svalagnabhāvāvaraṇo nīlīrāgaḥ satāṃ mataḥ yathāvalokyate caiṣa candrāvalimukundayoḥ  RUnm yathāprasannaviśadāśayā vividhamudrayā nirmitaṃpratāraṇam api tvayā guṇatayā sadā gṛhṇatī tathā vyavajahāra sā vrajakulendra candrāvalīsakhībhir api tarkitā tvayi yathā taṭasthety asau  RUnm atha śyāmārāgaḥbhīrutauṣadhisekādir ādyāt kiñcit muditātamisrārdhe māniny ahaha bhavatī taṃ mṛgayate  RUnm atha raktimārāgaḥ kusumbhamañjiṣṭhāsambhavo raktimā mataḥ  RUnm tatra kusumbharāgaḥkusumbharāgaḥ sa jñeyo yaś citte sajjati drutam anyarāgacchavivyañjī śobhate ca yathocitam  RUnm yathātvayy eva śravaṇāvadhi priyasakhī yā kṛṣṇabaddhāntarāyā dṛṣṭe bhujagepi tāvakabhujāsāmyāt pramodonmadā prekṣya tvāṃ puratodya kām api daśāṃ prātāsti seyaṃ tathāna jñāyeta yathā kim eṣa balavān rāgo virāgothavā  RUnm sadādhāraviśeṣeṣu kausumbhopi sthiro bhavet iti kṛṣṇapraṇayiṣu mlānir asya na yujyate  RUnm atha mañjiṣṭharāgaḥahāryonanyasāpekṣo yaḥ kāntyā varddhate sadā bhaven māñjiṣṭharāgosau rādhāmādhavayor yathā  RUnm yathādhatte drāg anupādhi janma vidhinā kenāpi nākampatesūtety āhitasañcayair api rasaṃ te cen mitho vartmane ṛddhiṃ sañcinute camatkṛtikaroddāmapramodottarāṃrādhāmādhavayor ayaṃ nirupamaḥ premānubandhotsavaḥ  RUnm yathā vā vidagdhamādhave mayā te nirbandhān murajayini rāgaḥ ātmapakṣavipakṣādibhedāḥ pūrvam udīritāḥ  RUnm yā bhāvāntarasambandhāj jāyante vividhā bhidāḥ aparā api bhāvānāṃ jñeyās tāḥ prajñayā budhaiḥ  RUnm atha anurāgaḥsadānubhūtam api yaḥ kuryān navanavaṃ priyam rāgo bhavan navanavaḥ sonurāga itīryate  RUnm yathā dānakelikaumudyām prapannaḥ panthānaṃ harir asakṛd asmannayanayorapūrvoyaṃ pūrvaṃ kvacid api na dṛṣṭo madhurimā pratīkepy ekasya sphurati mā kuru mohite tvam adhunā nyastāsya haste mayāsatyaṃ satyam asau dṛgaṅganam agād adyaivaa vidyunnibhaḥ  RUnm parasparavaśībhāvaḥ premavaicittyakaṃ tathā aprāṇiny api janmāptau lālasābhara unnataḥ vipralambhesya visphūrtir ity ādyāḥ syur iha kriyāḥ  RUnm atra parasparavaśībhāvo yathāsamārambhaṃ pārasparikavijayāya prathan natorapūrvā keyaṃ vām aghadamana saṃrambhalaharī manohastī bandhas tava yathābrūyās tvaṃ mathurādhvanīna mathurānāthaṃ tam ity uccakaiḥsandeśaṃ vrajasundarī kam api te kācin mayā prāhiṇot tatra kṣmāpatipattane yadi gataḥ svacchanda gacchādhunākiṃ kliṣṭām api visphuran atidurlabhaḥ vrajadevy ekasaṃvedyo mahābhāvākhyayocyate  RUnm varāmṛtasvarūpaśrīḥ svaṃ svarūpaṃ mano nayet  RUnm sa rūḍhaś cādhirūḍhaś cety ucyate dvividho budhaiḥ  RUnm tatra rūḍhaḥuddīptā sāttvikā yatra sa rūḍha iti bhaṇyate  RUnm nimeṣāsahatāsannajanatāhṛdviloḍanam kalpakṣaṇatvaṃ khinnatvaṃ tatsaukhyepy ārtiśaṅkayā  RUnm mohādyabhāvepy ātmādisarvavismaraṇaṃ sadā kṣaṇasya kalpaetyādyā yatra yogaviyogayoḥ  RUnm tatra nimeṣāsahatāyathā śrīdaśame gopyaś ca kṛṣṇam upalabhya cirād abhīṣṭaṃyatprekṣaṇe dṛśiṣu pakṣmakṛtaṃ śapanti dṛgbhir hṛdīkṛtam alaṃ parirabhya sarvāstadbhāvam āpur api nityayujāṃ durāpam  RUnm āsannajanatāhṛdviloḍanaṃ yathāsakhyaḥ prokṣya kurūn gurukṣitibhṛtām āghūrṇayantī śiraḥsvasthā viślathayanty aśeṣaramaṇīr āplāvya sarvaṃ janam gopīnām anurāgasindhulaharī sukhotsekārambhe nimiṣalavakalpām iva daśāṃmahākalpākalpāpy ahaha labhate kālakalanā  RUnm tatsaukhyepy ārtiśaṅkayā khinnatvamyathā śrīdaśame yat te sujātacaraṇāmburuhaṃ staneṣubhītāḥ śanaiḥ priya dadhīmahi karkaśeṣutenāṭavīm aṭasi tad vyathate na kiṃ svitkūrpādibhir bhramati dhīr bhavadāyuṣāṃ naḥ  RUnm mohādyabhāvepi sarvavismaraṇaṃyathā ekādaśe tā nāvidan mayy anuṣaṅgabaddhadhiyaḥ svam ātmānam adas tathedamyathā samādhau munayobdhitoyenadyaḥ praviṣṭā iva nāmarūpe  RUnm kṣaṇakalpatāyathā tatraiva tās tāḥ kṣapāḥ preṣṭhatamena nītāmayaiva vṛndāvanagocareṇa kṣaṇārdhavat tāḥ punar aṅga tāsāṃhīnā mayā kalpasamā babhūvuḥ  RUnm ādyaśabdād iha proktā kṛṣṇāvirbhāvakāritā sambhogabhede vispaṣṭaṃ sā purastāt pravakṣyate  RUnm atha adhirūḍhaḥrūḍhoktebhyonubhāvebhyaḥ kām apy āptā viśiṣṭatām api tat kuṭadvayaṃ rādhikāpremodyatsukhaduḥkhasindhubhavayor vindeta bindvor api  RUnm modano mādanaś cāsāv adhirūḍho dvidhocyate  RUnm tatra modanaḥmodanaḥ sa dvayor yatra sāttvikoddīptasauṣṭhavam  RUnm yathā lalitamādhave ātanvan kalakaṇṭhanādam atulaṃ stambhaśriyojjṛmbhitobhūyiṣṭhocchaladaṅkuraḥ phalitavān svedāmbumuktāphalaiḥ udyadbāṣpamarandabhāgavicalopy utkampavān vibhramairādhāmādhavayor suvilāsaḥ priyo varaḥ  RUnm tatra sakāntasya hareḥ kṣobhabharakāritā yathāhanta stambhakarambitā bhuvi kuror bhadrā sarasvaty abhūdbāṣpaṃ bhāskarajā mumoca tarasā satyābhraman narmadā bheje bhīṣmasutā ca varṇavikṛtiṃ gāmbhīryabhāg apy asaukṛṣṇodanvati rādhikādbhutanadīpremormibhiḥ saṃvṛte  RUnm premorusampadvatīvṛndātiśayitvaṃ yathāadvaitād girijāṃ harārdhavapuṣaṃ sakhyāt priyoraḥsthitāṃlakṣmīm acyutacittabhṛṅganalinīṃ satyāṃ ca saubhāgyataḥ mādhuryān madhureśajīvitasakhīṃ candrāvalīṃ ca kṣipanpaśyāruddha hariṃ prasārya laharīṃ rādhānurāgāmbudhiḥ  RUnm modanoyaṃ praviśleṣadaśāyāṃ mohano RUnm tatra kāntāśliṣṭepi harau mūrcchākāritvaṃyathā padyāvalyām ratnacchāyācchuritajaladhau mandire dvārakāyārukmiṇyāpi prabalapulakodbhedam āliṅgitasya viśvaṃ pāyān svedam ūhevṛndaṃ vṛndārakāṇāṃ pracuramudam amucann aśru vaikuṇṭhabhājaḥ rādhāyāś citram īśa bhramati diśi diśi premaniḥśvāsadhūmepūrṇānandepy uṣitvā bahir idam abahiś cārtam āsīd ajāṇḍam  RUnm yathā vāaurvastomāt kaṭur api kathaṃ durbalenorasā metāpaḥ prauḍho harivirahajaḥ sahyate tan na jāne niṣkrāntā ced bhavati hṛdayād yasya dhūmacchaṭāpibrahmāṇḍānāṃ sakhi kulam api jvālayā jājvalīti  RUnm bhramābhā kāpi vaicitrī divyonmāda itīryate  RUnm udghūrṇācitrajalpādyās tadbhedā bahavo matāḥ  RUnm tatra udghūrṇāsyād vilakṣaṇam udghūrṇā nānāvaivaśyaceṣṭitam  RUnm yathāśayyāṃ kuñjagṛhe kvacid RUnm citrajalpo daśāṅgoyaṃ prajalpaḥ parijalpitam vijalpojjalpasaṃjalpā avajalpobhijalpitam ājalpaḥ pratijalpaś ca sujalpaś ceti kīrtitāḥ  RUnm eṣa bhramaragītākhyo daśame prakaṭīkṛtaḥ  RUnm asaṅkhyabhāvavaicitrī camatkṛtisudustaraḥ api cec citrajalpoyaṃ manāk tad api kathyate  RUnm tatra prajalpaḥasūyerṣyāmadayujā yovadhīraṇamudrayā priyasyākauśalodgāraḥ prajalpaḥ sa tu kīrtyate  RUnm yathā madhupa kitavabandho mā spṛśāṅghriṃ sapatnyāḥkucavilulitamālākuṅkumaśmaśrubhir naḥ vahatu madhupatis tanmāninīnāṃ prasādaṃyadusadasi viḍambyaṃ yasya dūtas tvam īdṛk  RUnm atha kim iha bahu ṣaḍaṅghre gāyasi tvaṃ yadūnāmadhipatim agṛhāṇām agrato naḥ purāṇam vijayasakhasakhīnāṃ gīyatāṃ tatprasaṅgaḥkṣapitakucarujas te kalpayantīṣṭam iṣṭāḥ  RUnm atha ujjalpaḥhareḥ kuhakatākhyānaṃ garvagarbhitayerṣyayā sāsūyaś ca tadākṣepo dhīrair ujjalpa īryate  RUnm yathā divi bhuvi ca rasāyāṃ kāḥ striyas taddurāpāḥkapaṭarucirahāsabhrūvijṛmbhasya yāḥ syuḥ caraṇaraja upāste dhvāṅkṣavad yastad alam asitasakhyair dustyajas tatkathārthaḥ  RUnm atha abhijalpitambhaṅgyā tyāgaucitī tasya khagānām api khedanāt yatra sānuśayaṃ proktā tad bhaved abhijalpitam  RUnm yathā yadanucaritalīlākarṇapīyūṣavipruṭsakṛdadanavidhūtadvandvadharmā vinaṣṭāḥ sapadi gṛhakuṭumbaṃ dīnam utsṛjya dīnābahava iha vihaṅgā bhikṣucaryāṃ caranti  RUnm atha ājalpaḥjaihmyaṃ tasyārtidatvaṃ ca nirvedād yatra kīrtitam bhaṅyānyasukhadatvaṃ ca sa ājalpa udīritaḥ  RUnm yathā vayam ṛtam iva jihmavyāhṛtaṃ śraddadhānāḥkulikarutam ivājñāḥ kṛṣṇavadhvo hariṇyaḥdadṛśur asakṛd etat tannakhasparśatīvrasmararuja upamantrin bhaṇyatām anyavārtā  RUnm atha pratijalpaḥdustyajadvandvabhāvesmin prāptir nārhety anuddhatam dūtasammānanenoktaṃ yatra sa pratijalpakaḥ  RUnm yathā priyasakha punar āgāḥ preyasā preṣitaḥ kiṃvaraya kim anurundhe mānanīyosi meṅga nayasi katham ihāsmān dustyajadvandvapārśvaṃsatatam urasi saumya śrīr vadhūḥ sākam āste  RUnm atha sujalpaḥyatrārjavāt sagāmbhīryaṃ sadainyaṃ sahacāpalam sotkaṇṭhaṃ ca hariḥ pṛṣṭaḥ sa sujalpo nigadyate  RUnm yathā api bata madhupuryām āryaputrodhunāstesmarati sa pitṛgehān saumya bandhūṃś ca gopān kvacid api sa kathāṃ naḥ kiṅkarīṇāṃ gṛṇītebhujam agurusugandhaṃ mūrdhny adhāsyat kadā nu  RUnm atha mādanaḥsarvabhāvodgamollāsī mādanoyaṃ parāt paraḥ rājate hlādinīsāro rādhāyām eva yaḥ sadā  RUnm yathāāsṛṣṭer akṣayiṣṇuṃ hṛdayavidhumaṇidrāvaṇaṃ vakrimāṇaṃpūrṇatvepy udvahantaṃ nijarucighaṭayā sādhvasaṃ dhvaṃsayantam tanvānaṃ śaṃ pradoṣe dhṛtanavanavatāsampadaṃ mādanatvādadvaitaṃ naumi rādhādanujavijayinor adbhutaṃ bhāvacandramatrerṣyāyā ayogyepi prabalerṣyāvidhāyitā sadābhogepi tadgandhamātrādhārastavādayaḥ  RUnm atha ayogyepīrṣyāyathā dānakelikaumudyām viśuddhābhiḥ sārdhaṃ vrajahariṇanetrābhir aniśaṃtvam addhā vidveṣaṃ kim iti vanamāle racayasi tṛṇīkurvaty asmān vapur agharipor āśikham idaṃpariṣvajyāpāda mahati hṛdaye yā viharasi  RUnm sadābhogepi tadgandhamātrādhārastutiryathā śrīdaśame pūrṇāḥ pulindya urugāyapadābjarāgaśrīkuṅkumena dayitāstanamaṇḍitena taddarśanasmararujas tṛṇarūṣitenalimpantya ānanakuceṣu juhus tadādhim  RUnm yathā vāduṣkaraṃ kataradāli mālatīkomaleyam akarot tapaḥ purā hanta goṣṭhapatinandanopamaṃyā tamālam amalopagūhate  RUnm yoga eva bhaved eṣa vicitraḥ kopi mādanaḥ yadvilāsā virājante nityalīlāḥ sahasradhā  RUnm mādanasya gatiḥ suṣṭhu madanasyeva durgamā na nirvaktuṃ bhavec chakyā tenāsau munināpy alam  RUnm kiṃ carāgānurāgatām ādau snehaḥ prāpyaiva satvaram mānatvaṃ praṇayatvaṃ ca kvacit paścāt prapadyate  RUnm ataevātra śāstreṣu śrūyate rādhikādiṣu pūrvarāgaprasaṅgepi prakaṭaṃ rāgalakṣaṇam  RUnm sphuranti vrajadevīṣu parā bhāvabhidāś ca yāḥ tās tarkāygocaratyā na samyag iha varṇitāḥ  RUnm sādhāraṇyāṃ ratāv eva dhūmāyitatayā matāḥ jvalitās tu ratipremṇor dīptāḥ snehādipañcasu rūḍhe bhāve tathoddīptāḥ sudīptā mohanādiṣu  RUnm iyaṃ prāyikatā kintu śreṣṭhamadhyādibhārataḥ deśakālajanādīnāṃ kvāpy eṣāṃ syād viparyayam  RUnm ādyā premāntimāṃ tatrānurāgāntāṃ samañjasā ratir bhāvāntimāṃ sīmāṃ samarthaiva prapadyante  RUnm ratir narmavayasyānām anurāgāntimāṃ sthitim teṣv eva subalādīnāṃ bhāvāntām eva gacchati  RUnm iti śrīśrīujjvalanīlamaṇausthāyibhāvaprakaraṇam  atha śṛṅgārabhedaprakaraṇamsa vipralambhaḥ sambhoga iti dvedhojjvalo mataḥ  RUnm tatra vipralambhaḥyūnor ayuktayor bhāvo yuktayor vā tayor mithaḥ abhīṣṭāliṅganādīnām anavāptau prakṛṣyate sa vipralambho vijñeyaḥ sambhogonnatikārakaḥ  RUnm tathā coktamna vinā vipralambhena sambhogaḥ puṣṭim aśnute kāṣāyite hi vastrādau bhūyān evābhivardhate  RUnm pūrvarāgas tathā mānaḥ premavaicittyam ity api pravāsaś ceti kathito vipralambhaś caturvidhaḥ  RUnm tatra pūrvarāgaḥratir yā saṅgamāt pūrvaṃ darśanaśravaṇādijā tayor unmīlati prājñaiḥ pūrvarāgaḥ sa ucyate  RUnm tatra darśanātsākṣāt kṛṣṇasya citre ca syāt svapnādau ca darśanam  RUnm tatra sākṣātyathā padyāvalyām indīvarodarasahodarameduraśrīrvāso dravatkanakavṛndanibhaṃ dadhānaḥ āmuktamauktikamanoharahāravakṣāḥkoyaṃ yuvā jagadanaṅgamayaṃ karoti  RUnm citre yathā vidagdhamādhave śiśiraya dṛśau dṛṣṭvā divyaṃ kiśoram itīkṣitaḥparijalpanagirāṃ viśrambhāt tvaṃ vilāsaphalāṅkitaḥ śiva śiva kathaṃ jānīmas tvām avakradhiyo vayaṃniviḍabaḍavāvahnijvālākalāpavikāsinam  RUnm svapne yathāsvapne dṛṣṭvā sahacari saritkāsarī śyāmanīrātīre tasyāḥ kvaṇitamadhupā mādhavaīkuñjaśālā tasyāṃ kāntaṃ kapiśajaghano dhvāntarāśiḥ śarīrīcitraṃ candrāvalim api sa māṃ pātum icchann arautsīt  RUnm atha śravaṇamvandidūtīsakhīvaktrād gītādeś ca śrutir bhavet  RUnm tato vandivaktrāt yathāpaṭhati magadharājanirjayārthāṃsakhi virudāvalim atra vandivarye vada katham iva lakṣmaṇe tanutepulakakulena vilakṣaṇā kilāsīt  RUnm dūtīvaktrāt yathāāviṣkṛte tava mukunda mayā prasaṅgetārāvalī pulakitāṅgalatā natākṣī śuśrūṣur apy alaghugadgadaruddhakaṇṭhīpraṣṭuṃ tavākṣamata sā na kathāviśeṣam  RUnm sakhīvaktrāt yathāyāvad unmadacakoralocanāmanmukhāt tava kathām upāśṛṇot tāvad añcati dinaṃ dinaṃ sakhīkṛṣṇa śārad anadīrya tānavam  RUnm gītāt yathānayane praṇayann udaśruṇīmama sadyaḥ sadasi kṣitīśituḥ upavīṇayati pravīṇadhīḥkam udaśruḥ sakhi vaiṇiko muniḥ  RUnm puroktā yebhiyogādyā hetavo ratijanmani atra te pūrvarāgepi jñeyā dhīrair yathocitam  RUnm api mādhavarāgasya prāthamye sambhavaty api ādau rāge mṛgākṣīṇāṃ prokte syāc cārutādhikā  RUnm atra sañcāriṇo vyādhiḥ śaṅkāsūyā śramaḥ klamaḥ nirvedautsukyadainyāni cintānidrāprabodhanam  RUnm viṣādo jaḍatonmado mohamṛtyādayaḥ smṛtāḥ prauḍhaḥ samañjasaḥ sādhāraṇaś ceti sa tu tridhā  RUnm tatra prauḍhaḥsamarthaaratirūpas tu prauḍha ity abhidhīyate lālasādir iha prauḍhe maraṇāntā daśā bhavet tattatsañcāribhāvānām utkaṭatvād anekadhā  RUnm tathāpi prāktanair asya daśāvasthā samāsataḥ proktās tadanurodhena tāsāṃ lakṣaṇam ucyate  RUnm lālasodvegajāgaryās tānavaṃ jaḍimātra tu vaiyagryaṃ vyādhir unmādo moho mṛtyur daśā daśa  RUnm prauḍhatvāt pūrvarāgasya prauḍhāḥ sarvā daśā api  RUnm tatra lālasaḥabhīṣṭalipsayā gāḍhagṛdhnutā lālaso mataḥ atrautsukyaṃ capalatā ghūrṇāśvāsādayas tathā  RUnm yathātvam avasitān niṣkrāmantī punaḥ praviśanty asaujhaṭiti ghaṭikāmadhye vārāñchataṃ vrajasīmani agaṇitagurutrāsā śvāsān vimucya vimucya kiṃkṣipasi bahuśo nīpāraṇye kiśori dṛśor dvayam  RUnm yathā vā vidagdhamādhave dūrād apy anuṣaṅgataḥ śrutim ite tvannāmadheyākṣaresonmādaṃ madirekṣaṇā viruvatī dhatte muhur vepathum āḥ kiṃ vā kathanīyam anyadasite daivād varāmbhodharedṛṣṭe taṃ parirabdhum utsukamatiḥ pakṣadvayīm icchati  RUnm atha udvegaḥudvego manasaḥ kampas tatra niḥśvāsacāpale stambhaś cintāśruvaivarṇyasvedādaya udīritāḥ  RUnm yathā vidagdhamādhave cintāsantatir adya kṛntati sakhi svāntasya kiṃ te dhṛtiṃkiṃvā siñcati tāmram ambaram atisvedāmbhasāṃ ḍambaraḥ kampaś campakagauri lumpati vapuḥsthairyaṃ kathaṃ vā balāttathyaṃ brūhi na maṅgalā parijane saṅgopanāṅgīkṛtiḥ  RUnm atha jāgaryānidrākṣayas tu jāgaryā stambhaśoṣagadādikṛt  RUnm yathāśyāmaṃ kañcana kāñcanojjvalapaṭaṃ sandarśya nidrā kṣaṇaṃmām ājanma sakhī vimucya calitā ruṣṭeva nāvartate cintāṃ prohya sakhi prapañcaya matiṃ tasyās tvam āvartanenānyaḥ svāpnikataskaropaharaṇe śakto janas tāṃ vinā  RUnm atha tānavamtānavaṃ kṛśatā gātre daurbalyabhramaṇādikṛt  RUnm yathācyute valayasañcaye prabalariktatādūṣaṇavyayāya nihitormikāvalir api skhalaty añjasā niśamya muralīkalaṃ sakhi sakṛd viśākhe tanustavāsitacaturdaśīśaśikalā kṛśatvaṃ yayau  RUnm kaiścit tu tānavasthāne vilāpaḥ paripaṭhyate  RUnm yathāatrāsīn navanīpabhūruhataṭe kurvan vihāraṃ hariścakre tāṇḍavam atra mitrasahitaś caṇḍāṃśujārodhasi paśyantī latikāntare kṣaṇam ahaṃ vyagrā nilīya sthitaṃsakhyaḥ kiṃ kathayāmi dagdhavidhinā kṣiptāsmi dāvopari  RUnm atha jaḍimāiṣṭāniṣṭāparijñānaṃ yatra praśneṣv anuttaram darśanaśravaṇābhāvo jaḍimā sobhidhīyate atrākāṇḍepi huṅkārastambhaśvāsabhramādayaḥ  RUnm yathāakāṇḍe huṅkāraṃ racayasi śṛṇoṣi priyasakhīkulānāṃ nālāpaṃ dṛtir iva muhur niḥśvasiṣi ca tataḥ śaṅke paṅkeruhamukhi yayau vaiṇavakalāmadhulī te pāli śruticaṣakayoḥ prāghūṇikatām  RUnm atha vaiyāgryamvaiyāgryaṃ bhāvagāmbhīryavikṣobhāsahatocyate tatrāvivekanirvedakhedāsūyādayo matāḥ  RUnm yathā vidagdhamādhave pratyāhṛtya muniḥ kṣaṇaṃ viṣayato yasmin mano dhitsatebālāsau viṣayeṣu dhitsati tataḥ pratyāharantī manaḥ yasya sphūrtilavāya hanta hṛdaye yogī sumutkaṇṭhatemugdheyaṃ kila tasya paśya hṛdayān niṣkrāntim ākāṅkṣati  RUnm atha vyādhiḥabhīṣṭālābhato vyādhiḥ pāṇḍimottāpalakṣaṇaḥ atra śītaspṛhāmohaniḥśvāsapatanādayaḥ  RUnm yathādavadamanatayā niśamya bhadrāmadanadavajvalitā dadhe hṛdi tvām dviguṇitadavathuvyathāvidagdhāmurahara bhasmamayīva pāṇḍurāsīt  RUnm atha unmādaḥsarvāvasthāsu sarvatra tanmanaskatayā sadā atasmiṃs tu tad iti bhrāntir unmāda iti kīrtyate atreṣṭadveṣaniḥśvāsanimeṣavirahādayaḥ  RUnm yathā vidagdhamādhave vitanvānas tanvā marakatarucīnāṃ rucivatāṃpaṭān niṣkrāntobhūd dhṛtaśikhaṇḍo navayuvā bhruvaṃ tena kṣiptvā kim api hasatonmāditamateḥśaśī vṛtto vahniḥ param ahaha vahnir mama śaśī  RUnm atha mohaḥmoho vicittatā prokto naiścalyapatanādikṛt  RUnm yathānāsāśvāsaparāṅmukhī vighaṭite dṛṣṭī snuṣāyāḥ kathaṃhā dhik kṛṣṇatilān mamārpaya kare kuryām apāmārjanam ity ārohati karṇayoḥ parisaraṃ kṛṣṇeti karṇadvayekampenācyuta tatra sūtritavatī tvām eva hetuṃ sakhī  RUnm atha mṛtyuḥtais taiḥ kṛtaiḥ pratīkārair yadi na syāt samāgamaḥ kandarpabāṇakadanāt tatra syān maraṇodyamaḥ  RUnm tatra svapriyavastūnāṃ vayasyāsu samarpaṇam bhṛṅgamandānilajyotsnākadambānubhavādayaḥ  RUnm yathārādhā rodhasi ropitāṃ mukulinīm āliṅgya mallīlatāṃhāraṃ hīramayaṃ samarpya lalitāhaste praśastaśriyam mūrcchām āpnuvatī praviśya madhupair gītāṃ kadambāṭavīṃnāma vyāharatā hareḥ priyasakhīvṛndena sandhukṣitā  RUnm yathā vā vidagdhamādhave akāruṇyaḥ kṛṣṇo yadi mayi tavāgaḥ katham idaṃmudhā mā rodīr me kuru param imām uttarakṛtim tamālasya skandhe vinihitabhujavallarir iyaṃyathā vṛndāraṇye ciram avicalā tiṣṭhati tanuḥ  RUnm atha samañjasaḥbhavet samañjasaratisvarūpoyaṃ samañjasaḥ  RUnm atrābhilāṣacintāsmṛtiguṇasaṅkīrtanodvegāḥ savilāpā unmādavyādhijaḍatā mṛtiś ca tāḥ kramaśaḥ  RUnm tatra abhilāṣaḥvyavasāyobhilāṣaḥ syāt priyasaṅgam alipsayā svamaṇḍanāntikaprāptirāgaprakaṭanādikṛt  RUnm yathāyad iha sakhi subhadrāsakhyam ākhyāya dhūrtevrajasi pitur agārād devekīmandirāya racayasi bata satye maṇḍane ca prayatnaṃsphuṭam ajani tad antar vastu gūḍhaṃ tavādya  RUnm atha cintāabhīṣṭāvāptyupāyānāṃ dhyānaṃ cintā prakīrtitā śayyāvivṛttiniḥśvāsanirlakṣaprekṣaṇādikṛt  RUnm yathāniḥśvāsas te kamalavadane mlāpayatyoṣṭhabimbaṃśayyāyāṃ ca kraśimakalitā ceṣṭate dehayaṣṭiḥ dvandvaṃ cākṣṇor vikirati ciraṃ rukmiṇi śyāma ambhona śvobhāviny upayamavidhau śobhate vikriyeyam  RUnm atha smṛtiḥanubhūtapriyādīnām arthānāṃ cintanaṃ smṛtiḥ atra kampāṅgavaivaśyabāṣpaniḥśvasitādayaḥ  RUnm yathāplutaṃ pureṇāpāṃ nayanakamaladvandvam abhitodhṛtotkampaṃ sātrājiti kucarathāṅgadvayam api ślathārambhaṃ caitad bhujavisalayugaṃ tat tava manastaḍāgesmin kṛṣṇadviradapatir antar viharati  RUnm atha guṇakīrtanamsaundaryādiguṇaślāghā guṇakīrtanam ucyate atra vepathuromāñcakaṇṭhagadgadikādayaḥ  RUnm yathāyāntyas tṛṣṇāpi yuvatayo yeṣu ghūrṇāṃ bhajanteyāny ācamya svayam api bhavān romaharṣaṃ prayāti gandhaṃ teṣāṃ tava madhupate rūpasampanmadhūnāṃdūre vindan mama na hi dhṛtiḥ cittabhṛṅgas tanoti  RUnm ṣaḍudvegādayaḥ pūrvaṃ prauḍhe tasminn udāhṛtāḥ sāmañjasyād rater atra kintu tāḥ syur yathocitam  RUnm atha sādhāraṇaḥsādhāraṇaratiprāyaḥ sādhāraṇa itīritaḥ atra proktā vilāpāntāḥ ṣaḍdaśāntāś ca komalāḥ  RUnm atha abhilāṣoyathā prathamaskandhe etāḥ paraṃ strītvam apāstapeśalaṃnirastaśaucaṃ bata sādhu kurvate yāsāṃ gṛhāt puṣkaralocanaḥ patirna jātv apaity āhṛtibhir hṛdi spṛśan  RUnm cintādīnāṃ tathānyāsām ūhyā dhīrair udāhṛtiḥ  RUnm pūrvarāge prahīyeta kāmalekhasragādikam vayasyādikareṇātra kṛṣṇenāsya ca kāntayā  RUnm tatra kāmalekhaḥsa lekhaḥ kāmalekhaḥ syāt yaḥ svapremaprakāśakaḥ yuvatyā yūni yūnā ca yuvatyāṃ saṃprahīyate  RUnm nirakṣaraḥ sākṣaraś ca kāmalekho dvidhā bhavet  RUnm tatra nirakṣaraḥsuraktapallavamayaś candrārdhādinakhāṅkabhāk varṇavinyāsarahito bhaved eṣa nirakṣaraḥ  RUnm yathākisalayaśikhare viśākhikāyānakharaśikhālikhitoyam ardhacandraḥ dadhad iha madanārdhacandrabhāvaṃhṛdi mama hanta kathaṃ haṭhād viveśa  RUnm atha sākṣaramgāthāmayī lipir yatra svahastāṅkaiṣa sākṣaraḥ  RUnm yathā jagannāthavallabhesuiraṃ vijjhasi hiaaṃ lambhai maaṇo kkhu dujjasaḥ baliaṃ dīsasi saaladisāsuṃ dīsai maaṇo ṇa kuttābi  RUnm suciraṃ bidhyasi hṛdayaṃ labhate madanaḥ khalu duryaśo balīyaḥ dṛśyase sakaladiśāsu dṛśyate madano na kutrāpi bandhobjatantunā rāgaḥ kiṃ vā kastūrikāmasī pṛthupuṣpadalaṃ patraḥ mudrākṛt kuṅkumair iha  RUnm atha mālyārpaṇamsuśliṣṭāṃ nijaśilpakauśalabharavyāhāriṇīm adbhutāṃgoṣṭhādhīśvaranandanaṃ srajam imāṃ tubhyaṃ sakhi prāhiṇot ity ākarṇya giraṃ saroruhadṛśaḥ svedodabindūcchalādaṅgebhyaḥ kuladharmadhairyam abhitaḥ śaṅke bahir niryayau  RUnm kecit tunayanaprītiḥ prathamaṃ cintāsaṅgas tatotha saṅkalpaḥ nidrācchedas tanutā viṣayanivṛttis trapānāpa unmādo mūrcchā mṛtir ity etāḥ smaradaśā daśaiva syuḥ  RUnm ity ācakṣate evaṃ krameṇa vijñeyaḥ pūrvarāgo harer api nidarśanāya tatraikam udāharaṇam ucyate  RUnm yathāupāraṃsīd vaṃśīkalaparimalollāsarabhasādvisasmāra sphārāṃ vividhakusumākalparacanām jahau kṛṣṇas tṛṣṇāṃ sahacaracamūcārucaritesakhi tvadbhrūvyālīculukitacalaccittapavanaḥ  RUnm iti pūrvarāgaḥ atha mānaḥdampatyor bhāva ekatra sator apy anuraktayoḥ svābhīṣṭāśleṣavīkṣādinirodhī māna ucyate  RUnm sañcāriṇotra nirvedaśaṅkāmarṣāḥ sacāpalāḥ garvāsūyāvahitthāś ca glāniś cintādayopy amī  RUnm ahetor neti nety uker hetor yan māna ucyate asya praṇaya eva syān mānasya padam uttamam  RUnm tatra sahetuḥhetur īrṣyāvipakṣāder vaiśiṣṭye preyasā kṛte bhāvaḥ praṇayamukhyoyam īṛṣāmānatvam ṛcchati  RUnm tathā coktam śṛṅgāratilaka snehaṃ vinā bhayaṃ na syān nerṣyā ca praṇayaṃ vinā tasmān mānaprakāroyaṃ dvayoḥ premaprakāśakaḥ  RUnm ataeva harivaṃśe  ruṣitām iva tāṃ devīṃ snehāt saṅkalpayann iva bhītabhītotiśanakair viveśa yadunandanaḥ  RUnm rūpayauvanasampannā svasaubhāgyena garvitā abhimānavatī devī śrutvaiverṣyāvaśaṃ gatā  RUnm iti tatrāpi ca susakhyādi hṛdi yasyā virājate tasyā vipakṣavaiśiṣṭye na syād eva sahiṣṇutā  RUnm ataḥ satyāṃ vinānyāsāṃ susakhyāder abhāvataḥ śrutepi pārijātasya dāne māno na cābhavat  RUnm śrutaṃ cānumitaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tadvaiśiṣṭyaṃ tridhā matam  RUnm atha śravaṇamśravaṇaṃ tu priyasakhīśukādīnāṃ mukhād bhavet  RUnm tatra sakhīmukhāt yathāśaśimukhi mṛṣā jalpaṃ śrutvā kaṭhorasakhīmukhātpraṇayini harau mā viśrambhaṃ kṛthāḥ śithilaṃ vṛthā parihara manaḥklāntiṃ devi prasīda manorametava mukham anālocya preyān vanedya viśīryati  RUnm yathā vāahaha gahanā keyaṃ vārtā śrutau patitādya meviditam anṛtaṃ hāsyād brūṣe vimuñca kadarthanām sahacari kuto jīvaty asmin janepi janārdanodyutaru kusumaṃ tasyai hā dhik kṛtī vitariṣyati  RUnm śukamukhā yathāāste kācid dayitakalahā krūracetāḥ sakhī tekīro vanyaḥ sphuṭam iha yayā śyāmale pāṭhitosti atha vyarthe vihagalapite suṣṭhu viśrambhamāṇāmānārambhe na kuru hṛdayaṃ kātarosmi prasīda  RUnm anumitiḥbhogāṅkagotraskhalanasvapnair anumitis tridhā  RUnm atra bhogāṅkaḥbhogāṅko dṛśyate gātre vipakṣasya priyasya ca  RUnm tatra vipakṣagātre bhogāṅkadarśanaṃ yathākālindītaṭadhūrta cāṭubhir alaṃ nidrātu candrāvalīkhinnākṣī kṣaṇamaṅganād apasara kruddhāsti vṛddhā gṛhe kiñcid bimbitadhātupatramakarīcitreṇa tatrādhunāsarvā te lalitā lalāṭaphalakenodghāṭitā cāturī  RUnm priyagātre bhogāṅkadarśanaṃyathā vidagdhamādhave muktāntarnimiṣaṃ madīyapadavīm udvīkṣamāṇasyajāne keśarareṇubhir nipatitaiḥ śoṇīkṛte locane śītaiḥ kānanavāyubhir viracito bimbādhare ca vraṇaḥsaṅkocaṃ tyaja deva daivahatayā na tvaṃ mayā dūṣyase  RUnm tatra gotraskhalanamvipakṣasaṃjñayāhvānam īrṣyātiśayakāraṇam āsāṃ tu gotraskhalanaṃ duḥkhadaṃ maraṇād api  RUnm tena yathā bilvamaṅgalerādhāmohanamandirād upagataś candrāvalīm ūcivānrādhe kṣemam iheti tasya vacanaṃ śrutvāha candrāvalī kaṃsa kṣemam aye vimugdhahṛdaye kaṃsaḥ kva dṛṣṭas tvayārādhā kveti vilajjito natamukhaḥ smero hariḥ pātu vaḥ  RUnm yathā vāahaha vilasaty agre candrāvalī vimaladyutiḥkitava kalitā tārā sātra tvayā kva nu ṣoḍaśī timiramalinākāra kṣipraṃ vrajāruṇamaṇḍalāmama sahacarī yāvanmanyudyutiṃ na vimuñcati  RUnm atha svapnaḥharer vidūṣakasyāpi svapnaḥ svapnāyitaṃ mataḥ  RUnm tatra hareḥ svapnāyitam yathāśape tubhyaṃ rādhe tvam asi hṛdaye tvaṃ mama bahistvam agre tvaṃ pṛṣṭhe tvam iha bhavane tvaṃ girivane iti svapne jalpaṃ niśi niśamayantī madhuriporabhūt talpe candrāvalir atha parāvartitamukhī  RUnm vidūṣakasya yathāavañci caṭupāṭavair aghabhidādya padmāsakhītatas tvaraya rādhikāṃ kim iti mādhavi dhyāyasi niśamya madhumaṅgalād iti giraṃ puraḥ svapnajāṃvidūnavadanā sakhi jvalati paśya candrāvalī  RUnm atha darśanam yathāmithyā mā vada kandare sama sakhīṃ hitvā tvam ekākinīṃniṣkrāntaḥ pṛthusambhrameṇa kim api prakhyāpayan kaitavam dūrāt kiñcid añcitena rasanāśabdena sātaṅkayāniṣkramyātha tayā śaṭhendra puline dṛṣṭosi rādhāsakhaḥ  RUnm yathā vāsahacari parigumphya prātar evārpitāsīdbrajapatisutakaṇṭhe yā mayotkaṇṭhayādya api hṛdi lalitāyās tasthuṣī hanta hṛn medahati dahanadīptiḥ paśya guñjāvalī sā  RUnm atha nirhetuḥakāraṇād dvayor eva kāraṇābhāsatas tathā prodyan praṇaya evāyaṃ vrajen nirhetumānatām  RUnm ādyaṃ mānaṃ parīṇāmaṃ praṇayasya jagur budhāḥ dvitīyaṃ punar asyaiva vilāsabharavaibhavam budhaiḥ praṇayamānākhyaṃ eṣa eva prakīrtitaḥ  RUnm tathā coktam sarasvatīkaṇṭhābharaṇe aher iva gatiḥ premṇaḥ svabhāvakuṭilā bhavet ato hetor ahetoś ca yūnor māna udañcati  RUnm avahitthādayo hy atra vijñeyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ  RUnm tatra kṛṣṇasya yathāavyaktasmitadṛṣṭim arpaya puraḥ svalpopi mantur na mepatyur vañcanapāṭavād vrajapate jyotsnīniśārdhaṃ yayau śubhrālaṅkṛtibhir drutaṃ pathi mayā dūraṃ tataḥ prasthitesāndrā cāndram arundha bimbam acirād ākasmikī kālikā  RUnm yathā vāpuṣpebhyaḥ spṛhayā vilambitavatīm ālokya mām unmanāḥkaṃsāriḥ sakhi lambitānanaśaśī tūṣṇīṃ nikuñje sthitaḥ ātaṅkena mayā tadaṅghrinakhare kṣipte prasūnāñjalautasyālīkaruṣā bhruvaṃ vibhujatopy āvirbabhūva smitam  RUnm kṛṣṇapriyāyāḥyathā uddhavasandeśe tiṣṭhan goṣṭhāṅgaṇabhuvi muhurlocanāntaṃ vidhattejātotkaṇṭhastava sakhi Harirdehalīvedikāyām mithyāmānonnatikavalite kiṃ gavākṣārpitākṣīsvāntam hanta glapayasi bahiḥ prīṇaya prāṇanātham  RUnm yathā vāaham iha vicinomi tvadgiraiva prasūnaṃkathaya katham akāṇḍe caṇḍi vācaṃ yamāsi viditam upadhinālaṃ rādhike śādhi kenapriyasakhi kusumena śrotram uttaṃsayāmi  RUnm dvayor eva yugapad yathākuñje tuṣṇīm asi nataśirāḥ kiṃ cirāt tvaṃ murārekiṃ vā śyāme tvam api vimukhī maunamudrāṃ tanoṣi jñātaṃ jñātaṃ smitavimuṣite kāpi vāmāsti yogyākrīḍāvāde balavati yayā na dvayor eva bhaṅgaḥ  RUnm yathā vākuñjadvāri niviṣṭayos taraṇijātīre dvayor eva nautatrānyonyam apaśyatoḥ sakhi mudhā nirbandhataḥ klāntayoḥ haste drāg atha dāḍimīphalam abhinyaste mayā nistalaṃrādhām udbhidurasmitāṃ parihasan phullāṅgam āliṅgiṣam  RUnm nirhetukaḥ svayaṃ śāmyet svayaṃgrāhasmitāvidhiḥ  RUnm yathāroṣas tavābhūd yadi rādhikedhikastathāstu gaṇḍaḥ katham ucchvasity asau svanarmaṇetthaṃ durapahnavasmitāṃpriyām acumbat paśupendranandanaḥ  RUnm hetur yas tu śamaṃ yathāyogyaṃ prakalpitaiḥ sāmabhedakriyādānanatyupekṣārasāntaraiḥ  RUnm mānopaśamanasyāṅkā bāṣpamokṣasmitādayaḥ  RUnm tatra sāmapriyavākyasya racanaṃ yat tu tat sāma gīyate  RUnm yathājātaṃ sundari tathaym eva pṛthunā rādheparādhena mekintu svārasiko mamātra śaraṇaṃ snehas tvadīyo balī ity ākarṇya giraṃ harer natamukhī bāṣpāmbhasāṃ dhārayāsānaṅgotsavaraṅgamaṅgalaghaṭo pūrṇāvakārṣīt kucau  RUnm atha bhedaḥbhedo dvidhā svayaṃ bhaṅgyā svamāhātmyaprakāśanam sakhyādibhir upālambhaprayogaś ceti kīrtyate  RUnm tatra bhaṅgyā svamāhātmyaprakāśanaṃyathā vidagdhamādhave cañcanmīnavilocanāsi kamaṭhotakṛṣṭastanī saṅgatākroṅena sphuratā tavāyam adharaḥ prahlādasaṃvardhanaḥ madhyosau balibandhano mukharucā rāmās tvayā nirjitālabdhā śrīghanatādya mānini manasy aṅgīkṛtā kalkitā  RUnm athavedaṃ priyoktitvāt sāmodāharaṇaṃ bhavet nāyakasya svavacasā bhaṅgyāyaṃ bheda īryate  RUnm yathārūkṣā yan mayi vartase tvam abhitaḥ snigdhepi te dūṣaṇaṃtatrāste na hi kintu tat kila mamānaucityajātaṃ phalam yena svastaruṇīr upekṣya caramām apy āśrayantīr daśāṃpremārtaṃ vrajayauvataṃ ca sumukhi tvaṃ kevalaṃ sevyase  RUnm sakhyādibhir upālambhaprayogo yathākartuṃ sundari śaṅkhacūḍamathane nāsminn upekṣocitāsarveṣām abhayapradānapadavībaddhavrate preyasi ity ālībhir alakṣitaṃ murabhidā bhadrāvalī bheditānāsāgre varamauktikaśriyam adhād asrasya sā bindunā  RUnm atha dānamvyājena bhūṣaṇādīnāṃ pradānaṃ dānam ucyate  RUnm yathākāmo nāma suhṛn mamāsti bhavatīm ākarṇya matpreyasīṃhāras tena tavārpitoyam urasi prāpnotu saṅgotsavam ity unnamya karaṃ muradviṣi vadaty udbhinnasāndrasmitāpadmā mānavinigrahāt praṇayinā tenodbhaṭaṃ cumbitā  RUnm atha natiḥkevalaṃ dainyam ālambya pādapāto natir matā  RUnm yathākṣitiluṭhitaśikhaṇḍāpīḍam ārān mukunderacayati ratikāntastomakānte praṇāmam nayanajaladharābhyāṃ kurvatī bāṣpavṛṣṭiṃvaratanur iha mānagrīṣmanāśaṃ śaśaṃsa  RUnm atha upekṣāsāmādau tu parikṣīṇe syād upekṣāvadhīraṇam upekṣā kathyate kaiścit tūṣṇīmbhāvatayā sthitiḥ  RUnm tad dvayaṃ yathāsūnur vallabha eṣa vallavapates tatrāpi vīrāgraṇīstatrāpi smaramaṇḍalīvijayinā rūpeṇa vibhrājitaḥ sakhyaḥ samprati rūkṣatā pṛthur iyaṃ tenātra na śreyasedūre paśyata yāti niṣṭhuramanāḥ kā yuktir atrocitā  RUnm māne muhur nitibhir apy atidurnivārevācaṃyamavratam ahaṃ tarasāgrahīṣam bāṣpaṃ tato vikiratī nijagāda padmāpauṣpaṃ rajaḥ patitam atra dṛśor mameti  RUnm athavāprasādanavidhiṃ muktvā vākyair anyārthasūcakaiḥ prasādanaṃ mṛgākṣīṇām upekṣeti smṛtā budhaiḥ  RUnm yathādhammille navamālatī paricitā savye ca śabdagrahemallī sundari dakṣiṇe tu katarat puṣpaṃ tava bhrājate āghreyaṃ paricetum ity upahite vyājena nāsāpuṭegaṇḍodyatpulakā vihasya hariṇā candrāvalī cumbitā  RUnm atha rasāntaramākasmikabhayādīnāṃ prastutiḥ syād rasāntaram yādṛcchikaṃ buddhipūrvam iti dvedhā tad ucyate  RUnm tatra yādṛcchikamupasthitam akasmād yat tad yādṛcchikam ucyate  RUnm yathāapi gurubhir upāyair adya sāmādibhir yālavam api na mṛgākṣī mānamudrām abhāṅkṣīt harim iha parirebhe sā svayaṃgrāham agrenavajaladharanādair bhīṣitā paśya bhadrā  RUnm yathā vāupāyeṣu vyarthonnatiṣu bata sāmādiṣu sakhesakhīnāṃ cāturye gatavati ca sadyaḥ śithilatām viśākhāyāḥ kopajvaraharaṇamantrapratinidhiṃsacītkāraṃ rūkṣasvanitam akarod ukṣadanujaḥ  RUnm atha buddhipūrvambuddhipūrvaṃ tu kāntena pratyutpannadhiyā kṛtam  RUnm yathāpāṇau pañcamukhena duṣṭakṛmiṇā daṣṭosmi roṣād itivyājāt kūṇitalocanaṃ vrajapatau vyābhujya vaktraṃ sthite sadyaḥ projjhitaroṣavṛttir asakṛt kiṃ vṛttam ity ākulājalpantī smitabandhur āsyam amunā gāndharvikā cumbitā  RUnm yathā vānyastaṃ dāma kṛtāgasādya hariṇā dṛṣṭvā puro rādhayākṣiptenābhihataḥ sa tena kapaṭī duḥkhīva bhugnānanaḥ mīlann eva niṣedivān bhuvi tataḥ sadyas tayā vyagrayāpāñibhyāṃ dhṛtakandharaḥ sthitamukho bimboṣṭham asyāḥ papaudeśakālabalenaiva muralīśravaṇena ca vināpy upāyaṃ mānosau līyate vrajasubhruvām  RUnm tatra deśabalena yathāalaṅkīrṇaṃ candrāvalir alighaṭājhaṅkṛtibharaiḥpuro vṛndāraṇyaṃ kim api kalayantī kusumitam hariṃ ca smerāsyaṃ priyakatarumūle priyam itaḥskhalanmānā sakhyām adiśata satṛṣṇaṃ dṛśam asau  RUnm kālabalena yathāśaradi madhuramūrtiḥ paśya kānticchaṭābhiḥsnapayati ravikanyātīravanyāṃ sudhāṃśuḥ iti niśi niśamayya vyāhṛtiṃ dūtikāyāḥsmitarucibhir atānīt tatra rādhā prasādam  RUnm muralīśabdena yathāyadi roṣaṃ na hi muñcasina muñca mama devi nātra nirbandhaḥ phutkṛtividhūtamānaḥsa bhavatu vijayī harer veṇuḥ  RUnm yathā vāmānasyopādhyāyi prasīda sakhi rundhi me śrutidvandvam ayam uccāṭanamantraṃ siddho veṇur vane paṭhati  RUnm tāratamyaṃ tu mānasya hetoḥ syāt tāratamyataḥ syāl laghur madhyamaś cāsau mahiṣṭhaś cety atas tridhā  RUnm susādhyaḥ syāl laghur māno yatnasādhyasya madhyamaḥ duḥsādhyaḥ syād upāyena mahiṣṭhaḥ preyasāpy ayam  RUnm kṛṣṇe roṣoktayas tāsāṃ vāmo durlīlaśekharaḥ kitavendro mahādhūrtaḥ kaṭhoro nirapatrapaḥ  RUnm atidurlalito gopībhujaṅgo ratahiṇḍakaḥ gopikādharmavidhvaṃsī gopasādhvīviḍambakaḥ  RUnm kāmukeśas tamisraughaḥ śyāmātmāmbarataskaraḥ govardhanataṭāraṇyabāṭapāṭaccarādayaḥ  RUnm iti mānaḥ atha premavaicittyampriyasya sannikarṣepi premonmādabhramād bhavet yā viśleṣadhiyārtis tat premavaicittyam ucyate  RUnm yathāābhīrendrasute sphuraty api puras tīvrānurāgotthayāviśleṣajvarasampadā vivaśadhīr atyantam udghūrṇitā kāntaṃ me sakhi darśayeti daśanair udgūrṇaśasyāṅkurārādhā hanta tathā vyaceṣṭate yataḥ kṛṣṇopy abhūd vismitaḥ  RUnm yathā vā vidagdhamādhave samajani davād vitrastānāṃ kim ārtaravo gavāṃmayi kim abhavad vaiguṇyaṃ vā niraṅkuśam īkṣitam vyaraci nibhṛtaṃ kiṃ vāhūtiḥ kayācid abhīṣṭayāyad iha sahasā mām atyākṣīd vane vanajekṣaṇaḥ  RUnm vilāsam anurāgas tu kutracit kam api vrajam pārśve santam api preṣṭhaṃ hāritaṃ kurute sphuṭam  RUnm suṣṭhūdāharatā paṭṭamahiṣīgītavibhramam spaṣṭaṃ muktāphale caitad vopadevena varṇitam  RUnm iti premavaicittyamatha pravāsaḥpūrvasaṅgatayor yūnor bhaved deśāntarādibhiḥ vyavadhānaṃ tu yat prājñaiḥ sa pravāsa itīryate  RUnm tajjanyavipralambhoyaṃ pravāsatvena kathyate harṣagarvamadavrīḍā varjayitvā samīritāḥ  RUnm śṛṅgārayogyāḥ sarvepi pravāse vyabhicāriṇaḥ sa dvidhā buddhipūrvaḥ syāt tathiavābuddhipūrvakaḥ  RUnm atra buddhipūrvaḥdūre kāryānurodhena gamaḥ syād buddhipūrvakaḥ kāryaṃ kṛṣṇasya kathitaṃ svabhaktaprīṇanādikam  RUnm kiñcid dūre sudūre ca gamanād apy ayaṃ dvidhā  RUnm tatra ādyaḥdṛṣṭiṃ nidhāya surabhīnikurambavīthyāṃkṛṣṇeti varṇayugalābhyasena rasajñām śuśrūṣaṇe muralinisvanitasya karṇaucittaṃ mukhe tava nayaty ahar adya rādhā  RUnm atha dvitīyaḥbhāvī bhavaṃś ca bhūtaś ca tirvidhaḥ sa tu kīrtyate  RUnm tatra bhāvīyathā uddhavasandeśe eṣa kṣattā vrajanarapateḥ ājñayā gokule asminbāle prāto nagaragataye ghoṣaṇāmātanoti duṣṭam bhūyaḥ sphurati ca balādīkṣaṇaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ metena svāntaṃ sphuṭati caṭulam hanta bhāvyaṃ na jāne  RUnm bhavan yathā lalitamādhave bhānor bimbe tvaritam udayaprasthataḥ prasthitesauyātrānandīṃ paṭhati muditaḥ syandane gāndineyaḥ tāvat tūrṇaṃ sphuṭa khurapuṭaiḥ kṣauṇipṛṣṭaṃ khanantoyāvan nāmī hṛdaya bhavato ghoṭakāḥ sphoṭakā syuḥ  RUnm bhūto yathā uddhavasandeśe kāmaṃ dūre sahacari varīvarti yat kaṃsavairīna idam lokottaramapi vipaddurdinaṃ me dunoti āśākīlo hṛdi kila vṛtaḥ prāṇarodhī tu yo mesoyaṃ pīḍāṃ niviḍavaḍavāvahnitīvrastanoti  RUnm atra śrīyadusiṃhena preyasīhir amuṣya ca preṣaṇaṃ kriyate premṇā sandeśasya parasparam  RUnm yathā uddhavasandeśe soḍhavyaṃ te kathamapi balāccakṣuṣī mudrayitvātīvrottāpam hatamanasijoddāmavikrāntacakram dvitraireva priyasakhi dinaiḥ sevyatāṃ devi śavyeyāsyāmi tvatpraṇayacaṭulabhrūyugāḍambarāṇām  RUnm tathā padyāvalyām kālindyāḥ pulinaṃ pradoṣamaruto ramyāḥ śaśaṅkāṃśavaḥsantāpaṃ na harantu nāma nitarāṃ kurvanti kasmāt punaḥ sandiṣṭaṃ vrajayoṣitām iti hareḥ saṃśṛṇvatontaḥpureniḥśvāsāḥ prasṛtā jayanti ramaṇīsaubhāgyagarvacchidaḥ  RUnm atha abuddhipūrvaḥpāratntryodbhavo yas tu proktaḥ sobuddhipūrvakaḥ divyādivyādijanitaṃ pāratantryam anekadhā  RUnm yathā lalitamādhave ānītāsi mayā manorathaśatavyagreṇa nirbandhataḥpūrṇaṃ śāradapurṇimāparimalair vṛndāṭavīmaṇḍalam sadyaḥ sundari śaṅkhacūḍakapaṭaprāptodayenādhunādaivenādya virodhinā katham itas tvaṃ hanta dūrīkṛtā  RUnm cintātra jāgarodvegau tānavaṃ malināṅgatā pralāpo vyādhir unmādo moho mṛtyur daśā daśa  RUnm tatra cintāyathā haṃsadūte yadā yāto gopīhṛdayamadano nandasadanānmukundo gāndinyāstanayamanuvindan madhupurīm tadāmānkṣīccintāsariti ghanaghūrṇāparicayairagādhāyāṃ bādhāmayapayasi rādhā virahiṇī  RUnm atha jāgaraḥyathā padyāvalyāṃ yāḥ paśyanti priyaṃ svapne dhanyāstāḥ sakhi yoṣitaḥ asmākaṃ tu gate kṛṣṇe gatā nidrāpi vairiṇī  RUnm atha udvegaḥyathā haṃsadūte mano me hā kaṣṭaṃ jvalati kimahaṃ hanta karavaina pāraṃ nāvāraṃ kimapi kalayāmy asya jaladheḥ iyaṃ vande mūrdhnā sapadi tamupāyaṃ kathaya māṃparāmṛṣye yasmāddhṛtikaṇikayāpe kṣaṇikayā  RUnm atha tānavaṃ yathāudañcadvaktrāmbhoruhavikṛtir antaḥkaluṣitāsadāhārābhāvaglapitakucakokā yadupate viśuṣyantī rādhā tava virahatāpād anudinaṃnidāghe kulyeva kraśimaparipākaṃ prathayati  RUnm atha malināṅgatāhimavisaraviśīrṇāmbhojatulyānanaśrīḥkharamarudaparajyadbandhujīvopamauṣṭhī aghahara śaradarkottāpitendīvarākṣītava virahavipattimlāpitāsīd viśākhā  RUnm atha pralāpaḥyathā lalitamādhave kva nandakulacandramāḥ kva śikhicandrakālaṅkṛtiḥkva mandramuralīravaḥ kva nu surendranīladyutiḥkva rāsarasatāṇḍavī kva sakhi jīvarakṣauṣadhirnidhir mama suhṛttamaḥ kva bata hanta hā dhigvidhim  RUnm atha vyādhiḥyathā tatraiva uttāpī puṭapākato pi garalagrāmād api kṣobhaṇodambholer api duḥsahaḥ kaṭur alaṃ hṛnmagnaśūlyād apitīvraḥ prauḍhavisūcikānicayato py uccair mamāyaṃ balīmarmāṇy adya bhinatti gokulapater viśleṣajanmā jvaraḥ  RUnm atha unmādaḥbhramati bhavanagarbhe nirnimittaṃ hasantīprathayati tava vārtāṃ cetanācetaneṣu lutḥati ca bhuvi rādhā kampitāṅgī murāreviṣamavirahakhedodgārivibhrāntacittā  RUnm yathā vāadyākāṇḍikam aṭṭahāsapaṭalaṃ nirmāti gharmāmbubhākcītkāraṃ kurute camatkṛtiparā sotkaṇṭham ākasmikam ākrandaṃ vitanoti ghargharaghanodghoṣaṃ kilātarkitaṃrādhā mādhavaviprayogarabhasād anyeva tīvrād abhūt  RUnm atha mohaḥnirundhe dainyābdhiṃ harati gurucintā paribhavaṃvilumpaty unmādaṃ sthagayati balād bāṣpalaharīm idānīṃ kaṃsāre kuvalayadṛśaḥ kevalam idaṃvidhatte sācivyaṃ tava virahamūrcchāsahacarī  RUnm atha mṛtyuḥyathā haṃsadūte aye rāsakrīḍārasika mama sakhyāṃ navanavāpurā baddhā yena praṇayalaharī hanta gahanā sa cen muktāpekṣastvamapi dhig imāṃ tulaśakalaṃyadetasyā nāsānihitamidamadyāpi calati  RUnm pravāsavipralambhesmin daśās tās tā harer api atropalakṣaṇāyaikam udāharaṇam īryate  RUnm yathākrīḍāratnagṛhe viḍambitapayaḥphenāvalīmārdanetalpe necchati kalpaśākhicamarīramyepi rājñāṃ sutāḥ kintu dvāravatīpatir premabhedānām anubhāvatayā daśāḥ sādhāraṇyaḥ samastānāṃ prāyaśaḥ sambhavanty api  RUnm kintv atraivādhirūḍhasya mohanatvam apeyuṣaḥ asādhāraṇarūpās tu tatprasaṅge puroditāḥ  RUnm vipralambhaṃ paraṃ kecit karuṇābhidham ucire sa pravāsaviśeṣatvān naivātra pṛthag īritaḥ  RUnm iti vipralambhabhedāḥatha saṃyogaviyogasthitiḥharer līlāviśeṣasya prakaṭasyānusārataḥ varṇitā virahāvasthā goṣṭhavāmabhruvām asau  RUnm vṛndāraṇye viharatā sadā rāsādivibhramaiḥ hariṇā vrajadevīnāṃ virahosti na karhicit  RUnm tathā ca pādme pātālakhaṇḍe mathurāmāhātmyegogopagopikāsaṅge yatra krīḍati kaṃsahā  RUnm iti iti saṃyogaviyogasthitiḥatha sambhogaḥdarśanāliṅganādīnāṃ ānukūlyān niṣevayā yūnor ullāsam ārohan bhāvaḥ sambhoga ucyate  RUnm manīṣibhir ayaṃ mukho gauṇaś ceti dvidhoditaḥ  RUnm tatra mukhyaḥmukhyo sādhvasavrīḍitādibhiḥ upacārān niṣevete sa saṃkṣipta itīritaḥ  RUnm tatra nāyakena kṛtaḥyathā saptaśatyāmlīlāhituliaselo rakkhau vo rāhiātthaṇapphaṃse hariṇo paḍhamasamāgamasajjhasabebellio hattho  RUnm līlābhitulitaśailo rakṣatu vo rādhikāstanasparśe hareḥ prathamasamāgamasādhvasavevellito hastaḥ nāyikāyāḥ yathācumbe paṭāvṛtamukhī navasaṅgamebhūdāliṅgane kuṭilitāṅgalatā tadāsīt avyaktavāg ajani kelikathāsu rādhāmodaṃ tathāpi vidadhe madhusūdanasya  RUnm atha saṅkīrṇaḥyatra saṅkīryamāṇāḥ syur vyalīkasmaraṇādibhiḥ upacārāḥ sa saṅkīrṇaḥ kiñcit taptekṣupeśalaḥ  RUnm yathāsāsūyajalpitasudhāni samatsarāṇimanoparāmaramaṇīyadṛgiṅgitāni kaṃsadviṣaḥ sphuradamandamukhāny anaṅgavikrīḍitāni saha rādhikayā jayanti  RUnm yathā vāvaktraṃ kiñcid avāñcitaṃ vivṛṇute nātiprasādodayaṃdṛṣṭir bhugnataṭā vyanakti śanakair īrṣyāvaśeṣacchaṭām rādhāyāḥ sakhi sūcayaty aviśadā vāg apy asūyākalāṃmānantaṃ bruvatī tathāpi madhurā kṛṣṇaṃ dhinoty ākṛtiḥ  RUnm atha sampannaḥpravāsāt saṅgate kānte bhogaḥ sampanna īritaḥ dvidhā syād āgatiḥ prādurbhāvaś ceti sa saṅgamaḥ  RUnm tatra āgatiḥlaukikavyavahāreṇa syād āgamanam āgatiḥ  RUnm yathā uddhavasandeśe mā mandākṣaṃ kuru gurujanāddehalīṃ gehamadhyādehi klāntā yathā jagati cañcatā caṇakamuṣṭisampattayejanena patitā puraḥ kanakavṛṣṭir āsādyate  RUnm iti madhurarasaparipākavivekaḥ atha gauṇasambhogaḥchannaprakāśabhedena kaiścid eṣāṃ dvirūpatā iṣṭāpy atra na hi proktā nātyullāsakarī yataḥ  RUnm atha gauṇaḥsvapne prāptiviśeṣosya harer gauṇa itīryate svapno dvidhātra sāmānyaviśeṣatvena kīrtitaḥ  RUnm sāmānyaḥ sa tu yaḥ pūrvaṃ kathito vyabhicāriṣu viśeṣaḥ khalu jāgaryā nirviśeṣao mahādbhutaḥ  RUnm bhāvautkaṇṭhyemayo hy eṣa caturdhā pūrvavan mataḥ  RUnm tatra svapne saṅkṣipto yathāvihāraṃ kurvāṇas atha svāpnasamṛddhimānyathā lalitamādhave cirād adya svapne mama vividhayatnād upagateprapede govindaḥ sakhi nayanayor akṣaṇabhuvam gṛhītvā hā hanta tvaritam atha tasminn api rathaṃkathaṃ pratyāsannaḥ sa khalu puruṣo rājapuruṣaḥ  RUnm tulyasvarūpa evāyaṃ prodyan yūnor dvayor api ūṣāniruddhayor yadvat kvacit svapnopy abādhitaḥ  RUnm ataeva hi siddhānāṃ svapnepi paramādbhute prāptāni maṇḍanādīni kṛṣṇavartmavilasaddṛṣṭir viśākhāñcitā kandarpasya vidagdhatāṃ vidadhatI netrāñcalasya tviṣātvaṃ rādhe śivamūrtir ity urasi māṃ bhogīndram aṅgīkuru  RUnm vitathoktiḥyathā tatraiva asminn adrau kati na atha vṛndāvanakrīḍāsthalakamalamalīnāṃ stauti gītaiḥ padaṃ teradatatimatinamrā vandate kundarājī adharam anubhajantī lambate bimbamālāvilasati tava vaśyā paśya vṛndāṭavīyam  RUnm yamunājalakeliḥ yathāvyātyukṣīyudhi rādhayā ghanarasaiḥ paryukṣyamāṇasya temālyaṃ bhaṅgam avāpa vīra tilako yātaḥ kilādṛśyatām vaktrendau pratimācchalena śaraṇaṃ labdhaḥ sakhīṃ kaustubhastan mā bhūś cakito vaṃśīvastrapuṣpādihāritā  RUnm atha vaṃśīcauryamyathā padyāvalyāṃ nīcair nyāsād atha caraṇayor nūpura mūkayantīdhṛtvā dhṛtvā katakavalayāny utkṣipantī bhujānte mudrām akṣṇoś cakitaṃ śaśvad ālokayantīsmitvā smitvā harati muralīm aṅkato mādhavasya  RUnm atha vastracauryaṃ yathāchadāvalivṛtaiva naḥ sapadi kācid ekā vrajaṃpraviśya jaratīr ihānayatu ghorakarmoddhatāḥ ayaṃ guṇanidhis taror upari tābhir abhyarcyatāmumāvratakumārikāpaṭalacelapāṭaccaraḥ  RUnm atha puṣpacauryaṃ yathāayi jñātaṃ jñātaṃ harasi hariṇākṣi pratidinaṃtvam eva pracchannā mama sumanasāṃ mañjarim itaḥ cirād diṣṭyā manye vidhitsatha tad atra gires taṭeṣudurgeṣu hanta viṣameṣu raṇābhiyogam  RUnm atha kuñjādilīnatāyathā vidagdhamādhave śaṅke saṅkulitāntarādya niviḍakrīḍānubandhecchayākuñje vañjulaśākhinaḥ śaśimukhī līnā varīvarti sā no ced eṣa tadaṅghrisaṅgamavinābhāvād akāle kathaṃpuṣpāmodanimantritālipaṭalīstotrasya pātrībhavet  RUnm atha madhupānaṃ yathāmukhavidhum uditaṃ madhudviṣosaumadhucaṣake RUnm atha dyūtakrīḍājitvā dyūtapaṇaṃ daśaty aghahare gaṇḍaṃ mudā dakṣiṇaṃsā vāmaṃ ca daśeti tatra rabhasād akṣaṃ kṣipanty abhyadhāt ājñāṃ sundari te yatheti hariṇā vāme ca daṣṭe tataḥsaṃrambhād iva sā bhujālatikayā kaṇṭhe babandha priyam  RUnm atha paṭṭākṛṣṭiḥyathā lalitamādhave dhanyaḥ soyaṃ maṇir aviraladhvāntapuñje nikuñjesmitvā smitvā mayi kucapaṭīṃ kṛṣṭavaty unmadena gāḍhaṃ gūḍhākṛtir api tayā ivānilakampi cañcarīkaḥ  RUnm atha āśleṣo yathānavajāguḍavarṇayopagūḍhaḥsphuradabhradyutir etayonmadena harati sma harir hiraṇyavallīparivītāṅgatamālamaṅgalāni  RUnm atha nakhakṣataṃ yathāna kucāv imau gatijitā tayā hṛtaṃgajataḥ prasahya sakhi kumbhayor yugam kṣatam atra nāgadamano yad arpayatparamaṅgajāṅkuśavareṇa tatkṣaṇam  RUnm atha bimbādharasudhāpānaṃ yathāna hi sudhākarabimbasudhākaraṃkuru mukhaṃ karabhoru karāvṛtam adhararaṅgaṇam aṅga varāṅganepibatu nīpavanībhramaras tava  RUnm atha samprayogo yathādrāgdormaṇḍalapīḍanoddhuradhiyaḥ proddāmavaijātyayānirbandhād adharāmṛtāni pibataḥ sītkārapūrṇāsyayā kandarpotsavapaṇḍitasya maṇiatir ākrāntakuñjāntayāsārdhaṃ rādhikayā harer nidhuvanakrīḍāvidhir vardhate  RUnm vidagdhānāṃ mitho līlāvilāsena yathā sukham na tathā samprayogeṇa syād evaṃ rasikā viduḥ  RUnm yathābalena parirambhaṇe nakhaśikhābhir ullekhanaṃhaṭhād adharakhaṇḍane bhujayugena bandhakriyām dukūladalane hatiḥ kuvalayena kurvāṇayāratād api sukhaṃ harer adhikam ādadhe rādhayā  RUnm yathā vānarmotsekakalādṛgañcalacamatkārī bhruvor vibhramaḥsaṃvyānasya vikarṣaṇ caṭulatāṃ karṇotpalenāhatiḥ krīḍeyaṃ vrajanāgarīratiguror gāndharvikāyās tathābhūyiṣṭhaṃ suratotsavād api navāsvādaṃ vitene sukham  RUnm ataeva śrīgītagovinde pratyūhapulakāṅkureṇa niviḍaleśanimeṣeṇa cakrīḍākūtavilokitedharasudhāpāne kathākelibhiḥ ānandādhigamena manmathakalāyuddhepi yasminn abhududbhūtaḥ sa tayor babhūva suratārambhaḥ priyambhāvukaḥ  RUnm yathāgokulānanda govinda goṣṭhendrakulacandramaḥ prāṇeśa sundarottaṃsa nāgarāṇāṃ śikhāmaṇeḥ  RUnm vṛndāvanavidho goṣṭhayuvarāja manohara ity ādyā vrajadevīnāṃ preyasī praṇayoktayaḥ  RUnm atulatvād apāratvād āptosau durvigāhatām spṛṣṭaḥ paraṃ taṭasthena rasābdhir madhuro mayā oayam ujjvalanīlamaṇir gahanamahāghoṣasāgaraprabhavaḥ bhajatu tava makarakuṇḍalaparisarasevaucitīṃ deva oiti sambhogabhedāḥ iti śrīśrīujjvalanīlamaṇau śṛṅgārabhedaprakaraṇam sampūrṇoyaṃ śrīśrīlarūpagosvāmiprabhupādapraṇītaśrīśrīujjvalanīlamaṇir nāma granthaḥ
